<div class="col-a">
<div id="page-2356" class="elements-box post-2356 page type-page status-publish hentry">
<h5><span style="color: #339966;">ျမစိမ္းေတာင္ဆရာေတာ္ အရွင္ ဇာေနယ် ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား စုစည္းမွု (MP3)</span></h5>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h6><a href="https://www.thitsarparamisociety.com/uoakkahta-myaseintaung/" target="_blank"> ျမစိမ္းေတာင္ဆရာေတာ္၏တပည့္ ဦးဥကၠ႒၏တရားေတာ္မ်ား <span style="color: #ff0000;">&gt;&gt;&gt;Click Here</span></a></h6>
<h5><span style="color: #339966;">၂၀၁၈ခုႏွစ္၊ စကၤာပူႏိုင္ငံ၊ နဝမအႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ ျမစိမ္းေတာင္ဆရာေတာ္ (၉)ရက္</span></h5>
<h5><span style="color: #339966;">ဝိပႆနာအခ်ိန္ျပည့္ တရားစခန္း တြင္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span></h5>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/2018/MyaSeinTaung/2018-SINGAPORE/01.%201STDAY-081218-PM12%20UO.mp3"><span style="color: #ff9900;">အလုပ္ေပးတရားေတာ္ (၈.၁၂.၁၈) (12PM) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ဆရာေတာ္ ဦးဥကၠ႒</span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/2018/MyaSeinTaung/2018-SINGAPORE/02.%201STDAY-081218-PM3%20-UT.mp3"><span style="color: #ff9900;">ဝိပႆနာအေၾကာင္း သိေကာင္းစရာ တရားေတာ္ (၈.၁၂.၁၈)&nbsp; (2PM)&nbsp; (ဆရာေတာ္ ဦးသုႏၵရ)</span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/2018/MyaSeinTaung/2018-SINGAPORE/03.%201STDAY-081218-PM8-UO.mp3"><span style="color: #ff9900;">ဝိပႆနာနဲ႔ပတ္သက္ သိမွတ္ဖြယ္ရာမ်ား တရားေတာ္ အပိုင္း(၁)(၈.၁၂.၁၈) (8PM) </span></a></p>
<p><span style="color: #ff9900;">&nbsp;(ဆရာေတာ္ ဦးဥကၠ႒) </span></p>

<h5 class="style7 style9" align="justify"><span style="color: #339966;"><b> <span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One;">(၁၁) ၂၀၁၂ ျမစိမ္းေတာင္သႀကၤန္တရားစခန္းတြင္ ေဟာႀကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရား ေတာ္ မ်ား</span></b></span></h5>

<h5 class="style7" align="justify"><span style="color: #339966;"><b> (၁၀<span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One;">) ၂၀၁၂ ကိုးရက္ တရားစခန္း (Singapore, St.John’s Island) တြင္ ေဟာၾကား ေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span></b></span></h5>

<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2012_Retreat_MP3/02_22-01-2012_8am_%28WiPatThaNarThiSaYarMyar_2%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One; color: #ffcc00;"> ၀၂။ ၀ိပႆနာ သိစရာမ်ားတရားေတာ္-၂ (၂၂-၀၁-၂၀၁၂ မနက္ပုိင္း)</span></a></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2012_Retreat_MP3/03_22-01-2012_2pm_%28WiPatThaNarThiSaYarMyar_3%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One; color: #ffcc00;"> ၀၃။ ၀ိပႆနာ သိစရာမ်ားတရားေတာ္-၃ (၂၂-၀၁-၂၀၁၂ ေန ့လည္ပုိင္း)</span></a></p>

<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2012_Retreat_MP3/19_27-01-2012_8pm_%28KyoTinPyinSinBayYanSin-UThonDaRa%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One; color: #ffcc00;"> ၁၉။ ၾကိဳတင္ျပင္ဆင္ ေဘးရန္စင္ – ဦးသုႏၵရ (၂၇-၀၁-၂၀၁၂ ညပုိင္း)</span></a></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2012_Retreat_MP3/20_28-01-2012_8am_%28WiPatThaNarThiSaYarMyar_12%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One; color: #ffcc00;"> ၂၀။ ၀ိပႆနာ သိစရာမ်ားတရားေတာ္-၁၂ (၂၈-၀၁-၂၀၁၂ မနက္ပုိင္း)</span></a></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2012_Retreat_MP3/21_28-01-2012_2pm_%28WiPatThaNarThiSaYarMyar_13%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One; color: #ffcc00;"> ၂၁။ ၀ိပႆနာ သိစရာမ်ားတရားေတာ္-၁၃ (၂၈-၀၁-၂၀၁၂ ေန ့လည္ပုိင္း)</span></a></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2012_Retreat_MP3/22_28-01-2012_8pm_%28TaunPoGyiOoPaMar_2%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One; color: #ffcc00;"> ၂၂။ ေတာင္ပို႔ႀကီးဥပမာ-၂ (၂၈-၀၁-၂၀၁၂ ညပုိင္း)</span></a></p>
<h5 class="style7" align="justify"><b> <span style="color: #000080; font-family: Zawgyi-One;"><span style="color: #339966;">(၉) ၂၀၁၂ စကၤာပူ တရားပြဲမ်ားတြင္ ေဟာႀကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span> </span></b></h5>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2012_Retreat_MP3/29-01-2012_7pm_%28TaYarSeeMyinGyiLayMyo_1_%20Poh%20Ern%20Shinh%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One; color: #ffcc00;"> ၁။ တရားစည္းမ်ဥ္းႀကီးေလးမ်ိဳး-၁ – Poh Ern Shih Temple</span></span></a></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2012_Retreat_MP3/30-01-2012_7pm_%28%20TaYarSeeMyinGyiLayMyo_2_%20Poh%20Ern%20Shinh%20%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One; color: #ffcc00;"> ၂။ တရားစည္းမ်ဥ္းႀကီးေလးမ်ိဳး-၂ – Poh Ern Shih Temple</span></span></a></p>
<h5 class="style7" align="justify"><span style="color: #339966; font-family: Zawgyi-One;"><b>(၈) ရန္ကုန္ျမဳိ ့၊ ျပည္လမ္း၊ ၆မုိင္ခြဲ ေနအိမ္တြင္ ေဟာႀကားေသာတရားေတာ္</b></span></h5>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/Yangon/KoThaNarYwaeSakeMaNarSayNae_1.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One;"> <span style="color: #ffcc00;"> ၀၁။ ကုိယ္သာနာေစ စိတ္မနာေစနဲ ့တရားေတာ္</span></span><b><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One;"><br>
</span></b></span></a></p>
<h5 class="style7" align="justify"><b><span style="color: #000080; font-family: Zawgyi-One;"><span style="color: #339966;">(၇) ဆရာေတာ္ဘုရားႀကီး၏ ေမတၱာပုိ ့၊ ပရိတ္တရား၊ အေနကဇာတင္</span> </span></b></h5>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/PaYakeTayar/001MyittaPo.MP3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00; font-family: Zawgyi-One;"> ၀၁။ ေမတၱာပုိ ့နည္းမ်ားစုစည္းမႈ</span></a></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/PaYakeTayar/002PaYakeTayar.MP3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00; font-family: Zawgyi-One;">၀၂။ ပရိတ္တရား </span></a></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/PaYakeTayar/003AhNaKaZarTin.MP3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00; font-family: Zawgyi-One;">၀၃။ အေနကဇာတင္</span></a><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One;"><br>
</span></p>
<h5 class="style7" align="justify"><b> <span style="color: #000080; font-family: Zawgyi-One;"><span style="color: #339966;">(၆) ျမစိမ္းေတာင္ ဆရာေတာ္ႏွင့္ လယ္တီစံဆရာေတာ္ အရွင္ဓမၼပါလ အေမး အေျဖ</span> </span></b></h5>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><span style="color: #00ffff; font-family: Zawgyi-One;"> ၀၁။ လယ္တီစံဆရာေတာ္အရွင္ဓမၼပါလႏွင့္ အေမးအေျဖ </span></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><span style="color: #00ffff; font-family: Zawgyi-One;"><br>
( တရားျပသက္တန္း (၅)ႏွစ္ခန္ ့ရွိေသာ အရွင္ဓမၼပါလ မွ တရားအားထုတ္ရာ၊ တရားျပ ရာတြင္ႀကဳံေတြ ့ရေသာ အခက္အခဲ တခ်ဳိ ့ကုိ ျမစိမ္းေတာင္ဆရာေတာ္အား ေမးျမန္း ေလွ်ာက္ထားခ်က္)</span></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><span style="color: #00ffff; font-family: Zawgyi-One;">ႀကာခ်ိန္ ၄၂မိနစ္ေနာက္ပုိင္း အေမးအေျဖမ်ားမွာ ျမန္မာစကား ေျပာတတ္ေသာ အေမရိ ကန္ ႏုိင္ငံသား ဗုဒၶဘာသာ ရဟန္းတစ္ပါး ျမစိမ္းေတာင္ဆရာေတာ္ဘုရားထံသုိ ့ ေမးျမန္း ေလွ်ာက္ထားခ်က္မ်ား ျဖစ္သည္။)</span></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><span style="color: #339966;"><b><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One;">(၅) ျမစိမ္းေတာင္ဆရာေတာ္ တရားစခန္း ဆြမ္းစားမ်ားခ်ိန္တြင္ နာယူရေသာ ဆြမ္းစား အလုပ္ေပး တရား</span></b></span></p>
<p class="style7" align="justify"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/2011_retreat_MP3/017_MST_SwanSarSinChin_ALotePay.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00; font-family: Zawgyi-One;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၁။ ဆြမ္းစားအလုပ္ေပးတရား</span></span></a></p>
<h5 class="style7" align="justify"><span style="color: #339966;"><b><span style="font-family: Zawgyi-One;">(၄) ၂၀၁၁ (၂)ရက္ ေန ့တရားစခန္းႏွင့္တရားပြဲ(စကၤာပူ) တြင္ ေဟာၾကား ေတာ္မူ ေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span></b></span></h5>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/MyaSeinTaung/ALL/Dhamma%20Talks%20in%20Singapore%202011/002_MST_2011_DhammaTalk_SG.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00; font-family: Zawgyi-One;">၀၂။ ၀ိပႆနာတရားလြန္က်ဳိးမ်ား (၀၆-၀၂-၂၀၁၁) </span></a></span></p>

<div id="text-17" class="widget widget_text"><h3 class="widget-title">Feed Back</h3> <div class="textwidget"><p align="justify">ဓမၼမိတ္ေဆြ အေပါင္းတို ့ မိမိတုိ ့၏ တရားစခန္း အခက္အခဲမ်ား၊ နာၾကား အၾကံျပဳ လိုေသာ တရားဓမၼမ်ား ၊ ေမးျမန္းလိုေသာ ဓမၼေမးခြန္းမ်ား ၊ website ၾကည့္ရွုနာၾကားရာ ၌ အခက္အခဲမ်ား ျဖစ္ေပၚပါက ေအာက္ပါ Form တြင္ ျဖည့္စြက္၍ ေပးပို႔ အႀကံျပဳၾကပါရန္ ေမတၱာရပ္ခံအပ္ပါသည္။</p>

<script type="text/javascript">
		jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
			
		jQuery("#preloader-dqxzcq").fadeOut(1500, function () {
			jQuery("#ecf-form-dqxzcq").fadeIn(300);
			});
			
			$( '.ladda-button' ).ladda( 'bind' );

			$(function() {
				
						
				// Validation
				$("#form-dqxzcq").validate(
				{					
					// Rules for form validation
					rules:
					{
					name0:{required: true},email1:{required: true,email: true},message2:{required: true,minlength: 10},
							
									
					},
										
					// Messages for form validation
					messages:
					{
					name0:{required: "This field is required"},email1:{required: "This field is required"},message2:{required: "This field is required"}					},					
					// Do not change code below
					errorPlacement: function(error, element) {
						error.insertAfter(element.parent());
						},
						
					submitHandler: function (form) {
										 ecf_onsubmit(jQuery('.form-dqxzcq'));
						 
						 						 
						 },
						 
					invalidHandler: function (form) {	
					  	$.ladda( 'stopAll' );
					 	},
						 
					onkeyup: false,
					onfocusout: false,
					onclick: false
					
				});
			});	
			
			
			/* Form Submit ( Ajax ) */
			function ecf_onsubmit(form){	

				if(form.attr('action')=='#'){
					
					data = {};
					eldat = [];
					data['action'] = 'ecf_deliver_mail';
					data['formid'] = '12786';
					data['security'] = 'c0eb0b14f7';
		
		
						
					jQuery('input, textarea', form).each(function(key){
						
						items = {};
						
						if (typeof $(this).data('type') === 'undefined') { return true; }
						

						
						items['type'] = $(this).data('type');
						items['label'] = $(this).data('label');
						items['value'] = this.value;
						items['name'] = this.name;

						eldat.push(items);
							
						}); // END  form).each(function(key){
							

													

						data['allelmnt'] = JSON.stringify(eldat);

						submitForm();
				
					return false;
					
				} // End if(form.attr('action')=='#'){
				
			} // End ecf_onsubmit 
			
			// Start submitForm		
			  function submitForm() {
				  
				jQuery.ajax({
					url: 'https://www.thitsarparamisociety.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', 
					type: 'POST',
					dataType: 'json',
					data: data, 
					success: function(data) {
				
						if(data.Ok==true) {
									// success
							$("#form-dqxzcq").get(0).reset();	
								
							if(data.msg == 'redirect') {
								window.location = "http://";
								} else {
									notifyme('Your Message Submitted Successfully', 'n', 'success', 'left middle');
									}
		
							}
							else {
								$("#form-dqxzcq").get(0).reset();
								notifyme(data.msg, 'n', 'error', 'left middle');
								}
								
							$.ladda( 'stopAll' );	
									
							}
						});
						
										
					} // End submitForm
	
					
			// Notify	
			  function notifyme(msg, b, typ, pos) {
				  if (b == 'n') {
					  b = 'cf-submitteddqxzcq';
				  } else {
					 b = 'atcdqxzcq';
				  }
				  
				  $("#"+b).gnotify(msg,{
					  style: "nbootstrap",
					  elementPosition: pos,
					  className: typ
					  });
					  
					  msg = null;
					  typ = null;
					  
					}

		});		
		</script>

</fieldset>
